1. Parent-child travel recommends going to Manzhang Village, which is the same route as the Wild Elephant Valley. Children can catch fish, make handmade fans, make pottery, and there are local buildings, Dai cuisine, mango coconut milk glutinous rice, and roasted chicken. The baby caught fish and we ate roasted fish. It was a very happy stop! 
2. We chose a chartered tour, so we don‚Äôt have to worry about it. We basically ran to the famous attractions in Banna. It is especially suitable for bringing the elderly and children. The driver is also very good and patient throughout the journey. There are already a lot of people on the first day of the year. The entrance of Manting Park cannot be entered by cars. The driver also took a shortcut to try to let us walk less, which is very considerate. 
3. Dai flavor is not suitable for us. We chose to have two meals in the hotel. The native chicken pot is very delicious, with hot vegetables, which is absolutely amazing. There is also a stinky vegetable fried egg with stinky vegetables. The stinky vegetables are not stinky. There will be a portion of rice noodles or dry noodles every morning. 
4. There is a cat in the hotel, which is said to be a stray cat, but its fur is shiny and it doesn't look like a stray cat at all. The baby comes to feed it meat every day and names it "Xiaofu". The hotel's breakfast loses two slices of ham every day, which warms the cat's stomach and the baby's heart.
5. The day before we returned, we met a beautiful sister in the hotel. She was also going to take a flight. She gave the baby a balloon with a baby elephant. The baby was very happy. When we returned, we also gave the balloon to another child, and continued to pass on the beauty.
More fun, waiting for everyone to experience slowly.

Looking at the check-in reviews, the one-to-one service of the personal butler is indeed the highlight of this hotel, so when we were about to check in, the housekeeper Xiao Jia contacted us and was satisfied with the service of this hotel, but the next day We have to catch the 10:58 train to Kunming South and transfer to Dali. When I checked in, I confirmed to the front desk that there is a delivery service, and then confirmed with the housekeeper Xiao Jia. The housekeeper only told me to go at ten o'clock. According to the Gaode map, it takes about 20 minutes to drive, and it is almost enough to leave on time at 10 o'clock. Until the next day, the big silent incident happened in this hotel, which is famous for its reputation and service! I heard before that we can ask the butler to come and pick up our luggage in advance (because we are girls, the hotel has no elevator, it is difficult to move our luggage downstairs), I confirmed the delivery time with the butler at 9:45, whether I can go downstairs and wait, the butler only I said yes, I didn't offer to help with luggage. When I came to check in, I was very enthusiastic and went upstairs. When I left the store, my attitude really changed 720 degrees. But this is not the point that made us speechless, I called the front desk later, and another housekeeper took our luggage for us, and it didn't delay anything. The most speechless thing is that we waited in the lobby until 10 o'clock to deliver the train to the station before it came. For non-locals, we were very uneasy at that time, because we didn't know the situation of Banna Railway Station, including how long it took to check in at the station. We saw that there was still one hour left for the departure time, and immediately confirmed to the front desk. Another housekeeper who helped us pick up our luggage helped to call to confirm, saying that it might be a few minutes later, and we couldn't sit still until about 10:15, and repeatedly urged The front desk, the front desk confirmed to the delivery car again, and found that the housekeeper Xiao Jia who met me the day before did not arrange our delivery vehicle, which means that there was no car to send us at all! At this time, the front desk offered to drop the ticket for us. I checked with the front desk again whether our trains could catch up. If we couldn't catch up, we had to change the ticket. Because it was a transfer train, the two tickets had to be changed. The front desk said that it is estimated that we will not be able to catch up, so we changed the ticket to the closest train at 12:00, but the transfer time of the changed train in Kunming is only 20 minutes. If the vehicle is late, we will not be able to catch the transfer. Sure enough, when the Didi driver took us to Banna Station, the train we originally bought drove away in front of our eyes. On the way to the transfer, my girlfriend was dragging her luggage because of the bus, and she fell along with her luggage. Although he finally caught up with the car, his mood throughout the day was seriously affected by this series of events. The original play arrangements in Dali that night were all lost. Originally, the hotel industry is to earn reputation with service. Is it because it is on a show that people can't stand high? Don't travelers deserve to be taken seriously? The whole Yunnan was very impressed by this event! Once again, he also complained about the housekeeper Xiao Jia with his real name! I was very impressed with the professionalism of Podo Sen Oxy!
